local SmoothColorChangingScript = Instance.new("Script")
SmoothColorChangingScript.Name = "Smooth Color Changing Script"
SmoothColorChangingScript.Source = "r = 255\ng = 0\nb = 0\n\nwhile true do\n\twait(0.005)\n\t\n    while (r == 255 and g ~= 255) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tg = g + 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\twait(0.005)\n\tr = r - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\twhile (r ~= 0) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tr = r - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\n    while (g == 255 and b ~= 255) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tb = b + 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\twait(0.005)\n\tg = g - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\twhile (g ~= 0) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tg = g - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\t\n\twhile (b == 255 and r ~= 255) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tr = r + 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\twait(0.005)\n\tb = b - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\twhile (b ~= 0) do\n\twait(0.005)\n\tb = b - 1\n\tscript.Parent.Color = Color3.fromRGB(r,g,b)\n\tend\n\t\nend"
SmoothColorChangingScript.Parent = VisorGlow

local Ignore = {}
local LettersString = "qwertyuiopasdfghjklzxcvbnmQWERTYUIOPASDFGHJKLZXCVBNM_"
function RandomString(Length)
	local NewText = ""
	if typeof(Length) == "number" then
		for i=1,Length do
			local Selected = math.random(1,string.len(LettersString))
			NewText..=string.sub(LettersString,Selected,Selected)
		end
	else
		for i=1,math.random(50,100) do
			local Selected = math.random(1,string.len(LettersString))
			NewText..=string.sub(LettersString,Selected,Selected)
		end
	end
	return NewText
end
function ApplyRandomString(inst)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		inst.Name = RandomString()
		for i,v in pairs(inst:GetDescendants()) do
			if v then
				coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
					v.Name = RandomString()
				end))
			end
		end
	end))
end
function swait(Num)
	if typeof(Num) == "number" then
		if Num > 0 then
			for i=1,Num do
				game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
			end
		else
			game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
		end
	else
		game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
	end
end
function Swait(a) swait(a) end
Holder.Name,script.Name = RandomString(50),RandomString(50)
local UpdateWeld = function(w,p1)
	return p1*(w.C0*w.C1:Inverse())
end
function Clerp(a,b,c)
	return a:Lerp(b,math.clamp(c*Multiply,0,1))
end

function ChangeSkin()
	if Skin == 2 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin2.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin2.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin2.Limb:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin2.Limb:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin2.Limb:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin2.Limb:Clone(),Hair = Saves.Skin2.Hair:Clone(),Visor = Saves.Skin2.Visor:Clone(),VisorGlow = Saves.Skin2.VisorGlow:Clone(),Hood = Saves.Skin2.Hood:Clone(),Tail = Saves.Skin2.Tail:Clone(),Paw1 = Saves.Skin2.Paw1:Clone(),Paw2 = Saves.Skin2.Paw1:Clone(),Paw3 = Saves.Skin2.Paw2:Clone(),Paw4 = Saves.Skin2.Paw2:Clone(),Scarf = Saves.Skin2.Scarf:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin2.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin2.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin2.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin2.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin2.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.Neon,0
	elseif Skin == 3 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin3.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin3.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin3.RightArm:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin3.LeftArm:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin3.RightLeg:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin3.LeftLeg:Clone(),Hair = Saves.Skin3.Hair:Clone(),HeadGlow = Saves.Skin3.HeadGlow:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin3.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin3.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin3.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin3.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin3.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.fromRGB(99,95,98),Enum.Material.Granite,0
	elseif Skin == 4 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin4.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin4.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin4.Limb:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin4.Limb:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin4.Limb:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin4.Limb:Clone(),Hat = Saves.Skin4.Hat:Clone(),HeadGlow = Saves.Skin4.HeadGlow:Clone(),Pocket = Saves.Skin4.Pocket:Clone(),Tie = Saves.Skin4.Tie:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin4.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin4.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin4.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin4.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin4.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.Neon,0	
	elseif Skin == 5 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin5.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin5.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin5.Limb:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin5.Limb:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin5.Limb:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin5.Limb:Clone(),Mask = Saves.Skin5.Mask:Clone(),Eyes = Saves.Skin5.Eyes:Clone(),NeckFluff1 = Saves.Skin5.NeckFluff1:Clone(),NeckFluff2 = Saves.Skin5.NeckFluff2:Clone(),HeadFluff = Saves.Skin5.HeadFluff:Clone(),Ears = Saves.Skin5.Ears:Clone(),Tail = Saves.Skin5.Tail:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin5.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin5.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin5.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin5.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin5.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic,0	
	elseif Skin == 6 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin6.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin6.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin6.Limb:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin6.Limb:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin6.Limb:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin6.Limb:Clone(),Eyes = Saves.Skin6.Eyes:Clone(),Ushanka = Saves.Skin6.Ushanka:Clone(),Scarf = Saves.Skin6.Scarf:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin2.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin6.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin6.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin6.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin6.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.Neon,0

	elseif Skin == 8 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin8.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin8.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin8.RightArm:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin8.LeftArm:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin8.RightLeg:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin8.LeftLeg:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin8.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin8.LeftWing:Clone(),PunkRat = Saves.Skin8.PunkRat:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin8.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin8.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin8.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.fromRGB(86,66,54),Enum.Material.Granite,0
	elseif Skin == 9 then
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = Saves.Skin9.Head:Clone(),Torso = Saves.Skin9.Torso:Clone(),RightArm = Saves.Skin9.Limb:Clone(),LeftArm = Saves.Skin9.Limb:Clone(),RightLeg = Saves.Skin9.Limb:Clone(),LeftLeg = Saves.Skin9.Limb:Clone(),Hair = Saves.Skin9.Hair:Clone(),HeadGlow = Saves.Skin9.HeadGlow:Clone(),Scarf = Saves.Skin9.Scarf:Clone(),Hat = Saves.Skin9.TopHat:Clone(),RightWing = Saves.Skin9.RightWing:Clone(),LeftWing = Saves.Skin9.LeftWing:Clone(),GunBase = Saves.Skin9.GunBase:Clone(),GunAdditions = Saves.Skin9.GunAdditions:Clone(),GunNeon = Saves.Skin9.GunNeon:Clone(),homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.Neon,0
	else
		local New = Saves.PlayerAvatar:Clone()
		New.Name = RandomString()
		for i,v in pairs(New:GetChildren()) do
			if v.Name == "Accessory" then
				v.Name = RandomString()
				local NewTable = {Part = v,WeldTo = v:GetAttribute("WeldTo"),Offset = v:GetAttribute("HatOffset")}
				table.insert(Hats,NewTable)
			elseif v:IsA("Shirt") or v:IsA("Pants") or v:IsA("ShirtGraphic") or v:IsA("BodyColors") or v:IsA("CharacterMesh") then
				v.Name = RandomString()
			end
		end
		Character,MainColor,Material,Reflectance = {Head = New.Head,Torso = New.Torso,RightArm = New["Right Arm"],LeftArm = New["Left Arm"],RightLeg = New["Right Leg"],LeftLeg = New["Left Leg"],RightWing = New.RightWing,LeftWing = New.LeftWing,GunBase = New.GunBase,GunAdditions = New.GunAdditions,GunNeon = New.GunNeon,homero = Saves.homero:Clone()},Color3.new(),Enum.Material.Sand,0
		New.Parent = workspace
		FakeChar = New
	end
end
function ChangeVis()
	if VisSkin == 2 then
		Visualizer = {P1 = Saves.RoundedPart:Clone(),P2 = Saves.RoundedPart:Clone()}
	else
		Visualizer = {P1 = Saves.HPCylinder:Clone(),P2 = Saves.HPCylinder:Clone()}
	end
end
ChangeSkin()
ChangeVis()
local SoulAssets = {Trail = SoulPart.Trail,Particles = {Center = SoulPart.Particles.Center,Square = SoulPart.Particles.Square,Square2 = SoulPart.Particles.Square2,Particle = SoulPart.Particles.Particle,Smoke = SoulPart.Particles.Smoke}}
local SoulNums = {Square = 0,Smoke = 0}
local Theme,Distortion,SoundId,KillSound = Instance.new("Sound",Character.Torso),Instance.new("DistortionSoundEffect",nil),"rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..Mode..".m32","rbxassetid://6755792451"
Theme.Name = RandomString()
Theme.SoundId = SoundId
Theme.Looped = true
Theme.PlayOnRemove = false
Theme.Volume = 3
Theme.PlaybackSpeed = 1
Theme:Play()
Distortion.Parent = Theme
Distortion.Enabled = true
Distortion.Level = 0
Distortion.Priority = 0
local X,Y,Z = 0,0,0
local RootPart = CFrame.new(0,100,0)
local CamDir = Vector3.new()
local Pos,TouchingFloor,PosRot,Falling,Fall = CFrame.new(0,100,0),false,CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),false,0
local CameraCFrame,CameraAngles,RootAngles,RotAngles,PosAngles = CFrame.new(),{X=0,Y=0,Z=0,RevY=0},{X=0,Y=0,Z=0},{X=0,Y=0,Z=0},{X=0,Y=0,Z=0}
local Camera = nil
local InfoHolder,InfoText,InfoVis,InfoEnabled = nil,nil,nil,false
local SoulPos = Pos
function ApplyProperties(v)coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()v.Anchored,v.CanCollide,v.CanQuery,v.CanTouch = true,false,false,false;end))end
local BillBoards = {}
function Reset()
	Sine,VisSine = 0,0
	pcall(function()
		for i,v in pairs(Character) do
			if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
				pcall(function()v:Destroy()end)
			end
		end
	end)
	pcall(function()
		for i,v in pairs(Hats) do
			if typeof(v.Part) == "Instance" then
				pcall(function()v.Part:Destroy()end)
			end
		end
	end)
	pcall(function()Visualizer.P1:Destroy()end)
	pcall(function()Visualizer.P2:Destroy()end)
	pcall(function()table.clear(Character)end)
	pcall(function()table.clear(Visualizer)end)
	pcall(function()table.clear(Hats)end)
	pcall(function()table.clear(SoulAssets)end)
	pcall(function()Shield:Destroy()end)
	pcall(function()SoulPart:Destroy()end)
	pcall(function()Theme:Destroy()end)
	pcall(function()if FakeChar~=nil then FakeChar:Destroy()end;end)
	FakeChar = nil
	ChangeSkin()
	ChangeVis()
	Shield,SoulPart = Saves.Shield:Clone(),Saves.Soul:Clone()
	SoulAssets = {Trail = SoulPart.Trail,Particles = {Center = SoulPart.Particles.Center,Square = SoulPart.Particles.Square,Square2 = SoulPart.Particles.Square2,Particle = SoulPart.Particles.Particle,Smoke = SoulPart.Particles.Smoke}}
	for i,v in pairs(Character) do
		if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				if typeof(FakeChar) == "Instance" then
					if v == Character.Head or v == Character.Torso or v == Character.RightArm or v == Character.LeftArm or v == Character.RightLeg or v == Character.LeftLeg then else
						v.Name = RandomString()
					end
				else
					v.Name = RandomString()
				end
				v.CFrame = RootPart
				if v == Character.GunBase or v == Character.GunAdditions or v == Character.GunNeon then
					if HumanoidMode == true then
						if CannonOnBack == true or Attacking == true then
							v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
						else
							v.Parent = nil
						end
					else
						v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
					end
				elseif v == Character.RightWing or v == Character.LeftWing then
					if HumanoidMode == true and Skin == 1 then
						v.Parent = nil
					else
						v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
					end
				elseif v == Character.homero then
					if HumanoidMode == true and UseAnim == true and Moving == false and Falling == false and Attacking == false and Animation == 5 then
						v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
					else
						v.Parent = nil
					end
				else
					v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
				end
				ApplyProperties(v)
			end))
		end
	end
	for i,v in pairs(Hats) do
		if v.Part then
			v.CFrame = RootPart
			v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
		end
	end
	Visualizer.P1.Name,Visualizer.P2.Name,Visualizer.P1.Parent,Visualizer.P2.Parent,Visualizer.P1.Size,Visualizer.P2.Size,Visualizer.P2.Material,Visualizer.P2.Reflectance = RandomString(),RandomString(),workspace,workspace,Vector3.new(),Vector3.new(),Material,Reflectance;if Skin==1 then Visualizer.P2.Color=CurrentColor2;else Visualizer.P2.Color=MainColor;end
	Shield.Name,Shield.Size,Shield.Color,Shield.Material,Shield.Parent = RandomString(),Vector3.new(25,25,25),CurrentColor,Enum.Material.ForceField,nil
	ApplyRandomString(SoulPart)
	SoulPart.Parent = workspace
	Theme,Distortion = Instance.new("Sound",Character.Torso),Instance.new("DistortionSoundEffect",nil)
	Theme.Name = RandomString()
	Theme.SoundId = SoundId
	Theme.Looped = true
	Theme.PlayOnRemove = false
	Theme.Volume = 3
	Theme.PlaybackSpeed = 1
	Theme:Play()
	Distortion.Parent = Theme
	Distortion.Enabled = true
	Distortion.Level = 0
	Distortion.Priority = 0
	if LocalPlayer == Player then
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			local OldCamCFrame = Camera.CFrame
			Camera:Destroy()
			game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
			Camera = workspace["CurrentCamera"]
			Camera.CFrame = OldCamCFrame
		end))
		pcall(function()
			pcall(function()
				CameraPart:Destroy()
			end)
			CameraPart = Instance.new("Part", nil)
			CameraPart.Name,CameraPart.Anchored,CameraPart.Size,CameraPart.Transparency,CameraPart.CanCollide,CameraPart.CanQuery,CameraPart.CanTouch,CameraPart.CFrame = RandomString(),true,Vector3.new(),1,false,false,false,CFrame.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,1.5,0))
		end)
		pcall(function()
			pcall(function()
				InfoText:Destroy()
			end)
			pcall(function()
				InfoVis:Destroy()
			end)
			pcall(function()
				InfoHolder:Destroy()
			end)
			InfoHolder = Saves.InfoGui:Clone()
			InfoText,InfoVis = InfoHolder.TextFrame,InfoHolder.Visualizer
			ApplyRandomString(InfoHolder)
			InfoHolder.Enabled = InfoEnabled
			InfoHolder.Parent = PlayerGui
		end)
	end
	table.clear(Ignore)
end
function GunPos(Typ)
	if typeof(Typ) == "number" then
		if Typ == 1 then
			return CharCFrame.GunHandle*CFrame.new(0,1.305,-2.108)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-90),math.rad(-45))*CFrame.new(-0.983,-0.652,0)
		elseif Typ == 2 then
			return CharCFrame.GunHandle*CFrame.new(0,1.305,-2.108)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-90),math.rad(-45))*CFrame.new(-3.977,-3.645,0)
		else
			return CFrame.new()
		end
	end
end
if LocalPlayer == Player then
	pcall(function()
		CameraPart = Instance.new("Part",nil)
		CameraPart.Name,CameraPart.Anchored,CameraPart.Size,CameraPart.Transparency,CameraPart.CanCollide,CameraPart.CanQuery,CameraPart.CanTouch = RandomString(),true,Vector3.new(),1,false,false,false
	end)
	pcall(function()
		InfoHolder = Saves.InfoGui:Clone()
		InfoText,InfoVis = InfoHolder.TextFrame,InfoHolder.Visualizer
		ApplyRandomString(InfoHolder)
		InfoHolder.Enabled = InfoEnabled
		InfoHolder.Parent = PlayerGui
	end)
end
pcall(function() script:ClearAllChildren() end)

local function UST(D)if LocalPlayer == Player then return not game:GetService("UserInputService"):GetFocusedTextBox() and game:GetService("UserInputService"):IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType[D]) or false;end;end
pcall(function()Camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;end)
for i,v in pairs(Character) do
	if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			if typeof(FakeChar) == "Instance" then
				if v == Character.Head or v == Character.Torso or v == Character.RightArm or v == Character.LeftArm or v == Character.RightLeg or v == Character.LeftLeg then else
					v.Name = RandomString()
				end
			else
				v.Name = RandomString()
			end

			if v == Character.GunBase or v == Character.GunAdditions or v == Character.GunNeon then
				if HumanoidMode == true then
					if CannonOnBack == true or Attacking == true then
						v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
					else
						v.Parent = nil
					end
				else
					v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
				end
			elseif v == Character.RightWing or v == Character.LeftWing then
				if HumanoidMode == true and Skin == 1 then
					v.Parent = nil
				else
					v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
				end
			elseif v == Character.homero then
				if HumanoidMode == true and UseAnim == true and Moving == false and Falling == false and Attacking == false and Animation == 5 then
					v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
				else
					v.Parent = nil
				end
			else
				v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
			end
			ApplyProperties(v)
		end))
	end
end
Visualizer.P1.Name,Visualizer.P2.Name,Visualizer.P1.Parent,Visualizer.P2.Parent,Visualizer.P1.Size,Visualizer.P2.Size,Visualizer.P2.Material,Visualizer.P2.Reflectance = RandomString(),RandomString(),workspace,workspace,Vector3.new(),Vector3.new(),Material,Reflectance;if Skin==1 then Visualizer.P2.Color=CurrentColor2;else Visualizer.P2.Color=MainColor;end
Shield.Name,Shield.Size,Shield.Color,Shield.Material,Shield.Parent = RandomString(),Vector3.new(25,25,25),CurrentColor,Enum.Material.ForceField,nil
ApplyRandomString(SoulPart)
SoulPart.Parent = workspace
function ApplyColor(Instance_)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		pcall(function()
			if Instance_:IsA("BasePart") then
				while game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait() do
					if Instance_ == nil then
						return
					else
						if Instance_:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
							Instance_.Color = CurrentColor
						else
							return
						end
					end
				end
			elseif Instance_:IsA("TextLabel") then
				while game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait() do
					if Instance_ == nil then
						return
					else
						if Instance_:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
							Instance_.TextStrokeColor3 = CurrentColor
							Instance_.TextColor3 = CurrentColor
						else
							return
						end
					end
				end
			elseif Instance_:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or Instance_:IsA("Beam") then
				while game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait() do
					if Instance_ == nil then
						return
					else
						if Instance_:IsDescendantOf(workspace) then
							Instance_.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
						else
							return
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end))
end
function DestroyOnTime(Inst,Time)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		if Time >= 0 then wait(Time) end
		Inst:Destroy()
	end))
end
function KillEffect(CFram,Size)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		if KillEffectNum == 2 then
			local Part = Saves.Cube:Clone()
			table.insert(Ignore,Part)
			ApplyRandomString(Part)
			Part.CFrame,Part.Size = CFram,Size
			Part.Color = CurrentColor
			Part.Parent = workspace
			ApplyColor(Part)
			Sound(CFram.Position,KillSound,1+math.random(-50,50)*0.002,5)
			local SizNum,Posit = (Size.X+Size.Y+Size.Z),CFrame.new(Part.Position)
			local Sine2,Extra = math.random(0,1000),math.random(1,50)
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				while Part:IsDescendantOf(workspace) do
					Sine2=Sine2+1
					Posit = CFrame.new(Posit.Position)*CFrame.new((SizNum*.02)*math.cos(Sine2/30.251),(SizNum*.02)*math.cos(Sine2/37.451),(SizNum*.02)*math.sin(Sine2/35.762))
					Part.Size = Part.Size + Vector3.new(math.random(-50,50),math.random(-50,50),math.random(-50,50))*0.002
					Part.Position = Posit.Position
					game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
				end
			end))
			game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Part,TweenInfo.new(3*(1+(Extra*0.01)),Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,0,false,0),{Transparency = 1,Orientation = Vector3.new(math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360))}):Play()
			DestroyOnTime(Part,3*(1+(Extra*0.01)))
		else
			local Part = Saves.Cube:Clone()
			table.insert(Ignore,Part)
			ApplyRandomString(Part)
			Part.CFrame,Part.Size = CFram,Size
			Part.Color = CurrentColor
			Part.Parent = workspace
			ApplyColor(Part)
			Sound(CFram.Position,KillSound,1+math.random(-50,50)*0.002,5)
			local SizNum,Siz = (Size.X+Size.Y+Size.Z),Size
			local Sine2,Sp,Random_,Extra = math.random(0,1000),0.001,math.random(-50,50),math.random(1,50)
			game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Part,TweenInfo.new(1*(1+(Extra*0.01)),Enum.EasingStyle.Sine,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{Orientation = Vector3.new(math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360)),Position = CFram.Position+Vector3.new(math.random(-50,50),math.random(-50,50),math.random(-50,50))*(0.02*SizNum)}):Play()
			wait(1*(1+(Extra*0.01)))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				repeat
					Sine2,Sp = Sine2+1,Sp*1.2
					Part.CFrame = Part.CFrame:Lerp(CFrame.new(SoulPos.Position)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-Sine2*.1),math.rad(Sine2*.25),math.rad(-Sine2*.5)),math.clamp(Sp/10,0,1))
					Part.Size = Part.Size:Lerp(Vector3.new(),math.clamp(Sp/10,0,1))
					game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
				until Sp/10 >= 1
				Sound(Part.Position,"rbxassetid://7772692875",1+math.random(-50,50)*0.002,5)
				Part:Destroy()
				SoulAssets.Particles.Square2:Emit(1);SoulAssets.Particles.Particle:Emit(10)
			end))
		end
	end))
end
function Sound(Pos,SoundId,Pitch,Volume)
	local Holder = Instance.new("Part",game:GetService("SoundService"))
	table.insert(Ignore,Holder)
	Holder.Position = Pos
	Holder.Name = game:GetService("HttpService"):GenerateGUID(true)
	local Sound = Instance.new("Sound",Holder)
	Sound.Name = game:GetService("HttpService"):GenerateGUID(true)
	Sound.Playing = false
	Sound.SoundId = SoundId
	Sound.PlaybackSpeed = Pitch
	Sound.Volume = Volume
	Sound.PlayOnRemove = true
	DestroyOnTime(Holder,0)
	return Sound
end
function CameraShake(ShakePos_,Range_,Time_)
	if CameraShakes == true then
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			local ShakePos,Move,Time,ShakeCamera = ShakePos_,Range_,Time_,workspace["CurrentCamera"]
			local Dist = (ShakePos-ShakeCamera.CFrame.Position).Magnitude
			local Angles = {0,0}
			repeat
				Move = Move - (Time*0.01)
				Dist = (ShakePos-ShakeCamera.CFrame.Position).Magnitude
				Angles = {(-Move*.25)*(math.clamp(1-Dist/255,0,math.huge)),(Move*.25)*(math.clamp(1-Dist/255,0,math.huge))}
				ShakeCamera.CFrame = ShakeCamera.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(Angles[math.random(1,2)]),math.rad(Angles[math.random(1,2)]),math.rad(Angles[math.random(1,2)]))
				game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
			until Move <= 0
		end))
	end
end
function Beam(pos1,pos2)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			for i=1,5 do
				local Effect = Saves.Lightning2:Clone()
				table.insert(Ignore,Effect)
				Effect.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos1)
				local P1,P2,Particles,Beam = Effect.P1,Effect.P2,Effect.Particles.P1,Effect.Beam
				ApplyRandomString(Effect)
				Beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
				Beam.Enabled = true
				P1.CFrame,P2.CFrame = CFrame.new((math.random(-50,50)*0.01),(math.random(-50,50)*0.01),(math.random(-50,50)*0.01))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360))),CFrame.new((math.random(-50,50)*0.1),(math.random(-50,50)*0.1),(math.random(-50,50)*0.1))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360)))
				Effect.Parent = workspace
				ApplyColor(Beam);ApplyColor(Particles)
				Particles:Emit(1)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P1,TweenInfo.new(1,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{CFrame = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),math.rad(math.random(-45,45)))}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P2,TweenInfo.new(1,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{CFrame = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),math.rad(math.random(-45,45)))}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Beam,TweenInfo.new(1,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,0,false,0),{CurveSize0 = 0,CurveSize1 = 0,Width0 = 0,Width1 = 0}):Play()
				DestroyOnTime(Effect,1.1)
			end
		end))
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			for i=1,5 do
				coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
					local Effect = Saves.Lightning:Clone()
					table.insert(Ignore,Effect)
					Effect.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos1)
					local P1,P2,Particles,Beam = Effect.P1,Effect.P2,Effect.P2.P1,Effect.Beam
					ApplyRandomString(Effect)
					Beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
					Beam.Enabled = true
					P1.WorldCFrame,P2.WorldCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),0,math.rad(math.random(-360,360))),CFrame.new(pos2)*CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2).Rotation*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),0,math.rad(math.random(-360,360)))
					Beam.CurveSize0,Beam.CurveSize1 = math.random(-25,25),math.random(-25,25)
					Effect.Parent = workspace
					ApplyColor(Beam);ApplyColor(Particles)
					Particles:Emit(20)
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P1,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{WorldCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2)}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P2,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{WorldCFrame = CFrame.new(pos2)*CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2).Rotation}):Play()
					game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Beam,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,0,false,0),{Width0 = 0,Width1 = 0,CurveSize0 = 0,CurveSize1 = 0}):Play()
					DestroyOnTime(Effect,2)
				end))
			end
		end))
	end))
end
function Beam2(pos1,pos2)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		for i=1,5 do
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				local Effect = Saves.Lightning3:Clone()
				table.insert(Ignore,Effect)
				Effect.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos1)
				local P1,P2,Particles1,Particles2,Beam = Effect.P1,Effect.P2,Effect.P1.P1,Effect.P2.P1,Effect.Beam
				ApplyRandomString(Effect)
				Beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
				Beam.Enabled = true
				P1.WorldCFrame,P2.WorldCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),0,math.rad(math.random(-360,360))),CFrame.new(pos2)*CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2).Rotation*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-45,45)),0,math.rad(math.random(-360,360)))
				Beam.CurveSize0,Beam.CurveSize1 = math.random(-25,25),math.random(-25,25)
				Effect.Parent = workspace
				ApplyColor(Beam);ApplyColor(Particles1);ApplyColor(Particles2)
				Particles1:Emit(10);Particles2:Emit(10)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P1,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{WorldCFrame = CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2)}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(P2,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Elastic,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,0),{WorldCFrame = CFrame.new(pos2)*CFrame.lookAt(pos1,pos2).Rotation}):Play()
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Beam,TweenInfo.new(.25,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,0,false,0),{Width0 = 0,Width1 = 0,CurveSize0 = 0,CurveSize1 = 0}):Play()
				DestroyOnTime(Effect,2)
			end))
		end
	end))
end
function Teleport(pos1,pos2)
	local poss = {pos1,pos2}
	for i=1,2 do
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			for o=1,12 do
				local Part = Saves.Cube:Clone()
				table.insert(Ignore,Part)
				ApplyRandomString(Part)
				Part.CFrame,Part.Size,Part.Transparency = CFrame.new(poss[i])*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360)),math.rad(math.random(-360,360))),Vector3.new(o,o,o),.5
				Part.Color = CurrentColor
				Part.Parent = workspace
				ApplyColor(Part)
				local Extra = math.random(-50,50)
				game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(Part,TweenInfo.new(3*(1+(Extra*0.01)),Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.InOut,0,false,0),{Transparency = 1,Size = Vector3.new(),Orientation = Vector3.new(math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360),math.random(-360,360))}):Play()
				DestroyOnTime(Part,3*(1+(Extra*0.01)))
			end
			if i==1 then Sound(poss[i],"rbxassetid://4979952350",1+math.random(-50,50)*0.005,5)elseif i==2 then CameraShake(poss[i],10,100);Sound(poss[i],"rbxassetid://3848791288",5+math.random(-50,50)*0.005,5)end
		end))
	end
end
function MakeText(String,Color)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		game:GetService("Chat"):Chat(Character.Head,String,Color)
	end))
end
function Kill(Pos,Range)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		if LocalPlayer == Player and Damage == true then
			Remote:FireServer("Kill",{Pos = Pos,Range = Range})
		end
	end))
end
function Terrain(Pos,Range)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		if LocalPlayer == Player and Damage == true then
			Remote:FireServer("TerrainTool",{Pos = MousePos})
		end
	end))
end
function AttackOne()
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = true,false,true
	for i = 0,0.5,0.05 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(30)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(15),math.rad(0),math.rad(-30)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(0),math.rad(30)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(30),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	local Mous = MousePos
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		Sound(GunPos(2).Position,"rbxassetid://642890855",.45,10)
		Beam(GunPos(2).Position,Mous)
		Sound(Mous,"rbxassetid://192410089",.55,10)
		Kill(Mous,10)
		CameraShake(Mous,10,50)
	end))
	for i = 0,0.5,0.075 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(60)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(10),math.rad(0),math.rad(-60)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(160),math.rad(-20),math.rad(60)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(40),math.rad(5),math.rad(5)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = false,true,false
end
function AttackTwo()
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = true,false,true
	coroutine.wrap(function()
		for i = 0,2 do
			swait(12)
			Sound(Character.GunBase.Position,"rbxassetid://199145095",1,10)
		end
	end)()
	local doe = 0
	for i = 0,2,0.1 do
		swait()
		doe=doe+2
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(-10)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0 + ((1) - 1)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(25),math.rad(0),math.rad(-20)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(35),math.rad(-35),math.rad(20)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-20),math.rad(-5),math.rad(-10)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(doe * 22),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	for i = 0,1.5,0.1 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0 + ((1) - 1)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(15),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(175),math.rad(-10),math.rad(10)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-10),math.rad(-10),math.rad(-5)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		Sound(GunPos(2).Position,"rbxassetid://642890855",.45,10)
		Beam(GunPos(2).Position,GunPos(2).Position+Vector3.new(0,350,0))
		CameraShake(GunPos(2).Position+Vector3.new(0,350,0),10,50)
	end))
	for i = 0,.5,0.1 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0 + ((1) - 1)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(15),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(225),math.rad(-20),math.rad(20)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(-5),math.rad(0)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	for i = 0,.5,0.1 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0 + ((1) - 1)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(15),math.rad(0),math.rad(-5)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(175),math.rad(-10),math.rad(10)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(-5),math.rad(0)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = false,true,false
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		wait()
		for i=1,7 do
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				local Mous = MousePos
				Beam(Mous+Vector3.new(0,350,0),Mous)
				Sound(Mous,"rbxassetid://192410089",.55,10)
				Kill(Mous,10)
				CameraShake(Mous,10,50)
			end))
			wait(.5)
		end
	end))
end
function AttackThree()
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = true,false,false
	Sound(CharCFrame.Torso.Position,"rbxassetid://235097614",1.5,6)
	for i = 0,0.5,0.05 do
		swait()
		Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(-60)),1 / 3)
		Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0 * CFrame.new() * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(0),math.rad(60)),1 / 3)
		Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.25,0.5,-.25) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(0),math.rad(-60)) * Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.25,0.5,-.25) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(95),math.rad(0),math.rad(10)) * Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,1 / 3)
		if HipHeight > 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-0.5,-0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 + 9 * math.cos(Sine/74)),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 + 5 * math.cos(Sine/37)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15 - 9 * math.cos(Sine/54)),math.rad(-80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0 - 5 * math.cos(Sine/41)),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),0.7/3)
		elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
			Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(80),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-4),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
			Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(-70),math.rad(0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 3)
		end
		Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0,-.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),1 / 2)
	end
	local OldP = Pos.Position+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0)
	Kill(OldP,28)
	CameraShake(OldP,10,50)
	for i = 1,4 do
		if LocalPlayer == Player then
			Pos = CFrame.new(Pos.Position)*PosRot*CFrame.new(0,0,-25)
		end
		Kill(Pos.Position+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0),28)
	end
	RootPart = CFrame.new(Pos.Position+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0))*RootPart.Rotation
	Sound(Pos.Position+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0),"rbxassetid://642890855",.45,10)
	Beam2(OldP,Pos.Position+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0))
	Attacking,DoAnim,LookAt = false,true,false
end
function IgnoreParts(IgnoreTerrain)
	local Table = {}
	for i,v in pairs(Character) do
		if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
			if v:IsA("BasePart") then
				table.insert(Table,v)
			end
		end
	end
	for i,v in pairs(Hats) do
		if v.Part then
			if typeof(v.Part) == "Instance" then
				if v.Part:IsA("BasePart") then
					table.insert(Table,v.Part)
				end
			end
		end
	end
	for i,v in pairs(Ignore) do
		if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
			if v:IsA("BasePart") then
				table.insert(Table,v)
			end
		end
	end
	table.insert(Table,Visualizer.P1);table.insert(Table,Visualizer.P2);table.insert(Table,Shield);table.insert(Table,SoulPart);if LocalPlayer == Player then table.insert(Table,CameraPart);end;if IgnoreTerrain == true then table.insert(Table,workspace["Terrain"])end
	return Table
end
function UpdateTheme()
	local OldTheme = SoundId
	if UseAnim == false then
		if OldTheme == "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32" then else
			Remote:FireServer("UpdateTheme",{SoundId = "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32"})
		end
	else
		if HumanoidMode == false and UseAnim == true then
			if OldTheme == "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32" then else
				Remote:FireServer("UpdateTheme",{SoundId = "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32"})
			end
		elseif HumanoidMode == true and UseAnim == true then
			if Animation == 3 then
				if OldTheme == "rbxasset://MLCv5/Emotes/Potato/"..tostring(math.random(0,6))..".m32" then else
					Remote:FireServer("UpdateTheme",{SoundId = "rbxasset://MLCv5/Emotes/Potato/"..tostring(math.random(0,6))..".m32"})
				end
			elseif Animation == 0 then
				if OldTheme == "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32" then else
					Remote:FireServer("UpdateTheme",{SoundId = "rbxasset://MLCv5/Modes/"..tostring(Mode)..".m32"})
				end
			elseif Animation > 0 then
				if OldTheme == "rbxasset://MLCv5/Emotes/"..tostring(Animation)..".m32" then else
					Remote:FireServer("UpdateTheme",{SoundId = "rbxasset://MLCv5/Emotes/"..tostring(Animation)..".m32"})
				end
			end
		end
	end
end
function Void(v)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		v.Anchored,v.CFrame = true,CFrame.new(9e125,-9e125,9e125)
		table.insert(VoidTable,v)
		local CCF,CA
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			CCF = v:GetPropertyChangedSignal("CFrame"):Connect(function()
				if table.find(VoidTable,v) then
					coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
						v.CFrame,v.Anchored = CFrame.new(9e125,-9e125,9e125),true
					end))
				else
					CCF:Disconnect()
				end
			end)
		end))
		coroutine.create(coroutine.create(function()
			CA = v:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Anchored"):Connect(function()
				if table.find(VoidTable,v) then
					coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
						v.CFrame,v.Anchored = CFrame.new(9e125,-9e125,9e125),true
					end))
				else
					CA:Disconnect()
				end
			end)
		end))
	end))
end
function CheckP(_)
	local Bool = false
	if _:IsA("BasePart") then
		local v,Num=_,0
		if table.find(VoidTable2.ClassName,v.ClassName) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.Locked,v.Locked) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.Size,v.Size) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.Anchored,v.Anchored) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.CanCollide,v.CanCollide) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.CanQuery,v.CanQuery) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.CanTouch,v.CanTouch) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(VoidTable2.CastShadow,v.CastShadow) then Num=Num+1;end
		if table.find(IgnoreParts(true),v) or table.find(Ignore,v)then Num=0;end
		if Num >= 8 then
			Bool = true
		end
	end
	return Bool
end
function InsertP(v)
	if v:IsA("BasePart") then
		local Continue=true;if table.find(IgnoreParts(true),v) or table.find(Ignore,v)then Continue=false;end
		if Continue == true then
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.ClassName,v.ClassName) then table.insert(VoidTable2.ClassName,v.ClassName);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.Locked,v.Locked) then table.insert(VoidTable2.Locked,v.Locked);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.Size,v.Size) then table.insert(VoidTable2.Size,v.Size);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.Anchored,v.Anchored) then table.insert(VoidTable2.Anchored,v.Anchored);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.CanCollide,v.CanCollide) then table.insert(VoidTable2.CanCollide,v.CanCollide);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.CanQuery,v.CanQuery) then table.insert(VoidTable2.CanQuery,v.CanQuery);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.CanTouch,v.CanTouch) then table.insert(VoidTable2.CanTouch,v.CanTouch);end
			if not table.find(VoidTable2.CastShadow,v.CastShadow) then table.insert(VoidTable2.CastShadow,v.CastShadow);end
		end
	end
end
if LocalPlayer == Player then
	Keys=game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(k,w)
		if w == false then
			if k.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 and DisableKeys == false then
				Remote:FireServer("Function","Attack1")
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Y and DisableKeys == false then
				Remote:FireServer("Function","Attack2")
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Z and DisableKeys == false then
				Remote:FireServer("Function","Attack3")
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.P then
				Pos,RootPart,Fall = CFrame.new(0,100,0),CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0,103+HipHeight,0))*RootPart.Rotation,0
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.T then
				local OldPos,MousPos = Pos.Position,MousePos
				Pos,RootPart,Fall = CFrame.new(MousPos)*Pos.Rotation,CFrame.new(MousPos+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0))*RootPart.Rotation,0
				Teleport(OldPos+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0),MousPos+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0))
				Remote:FireServer("TPEffect",{Start = OldPos+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0),End = MousPos+Vector3.new(0,3+HipHeight,0)})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
				Flying = not Flying
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.B then
				HumanoidMode = not HumanoidMode
				if HumanoidMode==false then UseAnim = false;end
				UpdateTheme()
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.E and HumanoidMode == true then
				UseAnim = not UseAnim
				UpdateTheme()
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.One then
				Remote:FireServer("ClearTable",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Two then
				LookAtCamera = not LookAtCamera
				if LookAtCamera == true then
					MakeText("LookAt Enabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif LookAtCamera == false then
					MakeText("LookAt Disabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Three and HumanoidMode == true then
				CannonOnBack = not CannonOnBack
				if CannonOnBack == true then
					MakeText("Cannon Visible",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif CannonOnBack == false then
					MakeText("Cannon Invisible",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.K then
				Remote:FireServer("KillType",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.L then
				Remote:FireServer("DamageType",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
				Remote:FireServer("DamageBoolean",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.V then
				VisEnabled = not VisEnabled
				if VisEnabled == true then
					MakeText("Visualizer Enabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif VisEnabled == false then
					MakeText("Visualizer Disabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.J and DisableKeys == false then
				Remote:FireServer("ShieldEnabled",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
				Remote:FireServer("Reset",{})
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.M then
				if UseAnim == false then
					local LastMode = Mode
					Mode=math.clamp(Mode+1,0,13)
					if Mode == LastMode then else
						UpdateTheme()
					end
				else
					local LastAnim = Animation
					Animation=math.clamp(Animation+1,0,5)
					if LastAnim == Animation then else
						UpdateTheme()
					end
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.N then
				if UseAnim == false then
					local LastMode = Mode
					Mode=math.clamp(Mode-1,0,13)
					if Mode == LastMode then else
						UpdateTheme()
					end
				else
					local LastAnim = Animation
					Animation=math.clamp(Animation-1,0,5)
					if LastAnim == Animation then else
						UpdateTheme()
					end
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.G then
				InfoEnabled = not InfoEnabled
				if InfoEnabled == true then
					MakeText("Info Visible",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif InfoEnabled == false then
					MakeText("Info Hidden",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.X then
				CameraShakes = not CameraShakes
				if CameraShakes == true then
					MakeText("CameraShake Enabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif CameraShakes == false then
					MakeText("CameraShake Disabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			elseif k.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.C then
				TerrainTool = not TerrainTool
				DisableKeys = TerrainTool
				if TerrainTool == true then
					MakeText("TerrainTool Enabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				elseif TerrainTool == false then
					MakeText("TerrainTool Disabled",Enum.ChatColor.Green)
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end
function ConnectR(Inst)
	RFunction=Inst.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(typ,thing)
		if typ == "Character" then
			if LocalPlayer == Player then else
				Pos,PosRot,Sine,Moving,Falling,Fall,Flying,HumanoidMode,Mode,HipHeight,MousePos,VisEnabled,UseAnim,Animation,CameraShakes,TouchingFloor,CannonOnBack,LookAtCamera,CameraCFrame,CameraAngles = thing.Pos,thing.PosRot,thing.Sine,thing.Moving,thing.Falling,thing.Fall,thing.Flying,thing.HumanoidMode,thing.Mode,thing.HipHeight,thing.MousePos,thing.VisEnabled,thing.UseAnim,thing.Animation,thing.CameraShakes,thing.TouchingFloor,thing.CannonOnBack,thing.LookAtCamera,thing.CameraCFrame,thing.CameraAngles
			end
			ShieldEnabled,SoundId,KillSound,Damage,DamageType,KillType,Skin,VisSkin,CustomColorBoolean,CustomColor,CustomColor2,KillEffectNum = thing.ShieldEnabled,thing.SoundId,thing.KillSound,thing.Damage,thing.DamageType,thing.KillType,thing.Skin,thing.VisSkin,thing.CustomColorBoolean,thing.CustomColor,thing.CustomColor2,thing.KillEffect
		elseif typ == "MakeText" then
			if thing.ClientSide == true then
				if LocalPlayer == Player then
					MakeText(thing.Text,thing.Color)
				end
			elseif thing.ClientSide == false then
				MakeText(thing.Text,thing.Color)
			end
		elseif typ == "Function" then
			if thing == "Attack1" and Attacking == false then
				AttackOne()
			elseif thing == "Attack2" and Attacking == false then
				AttackTwo()
			elseif thing == "Attack3" and Attacking == false then
				AttackThree()
			end
		elseif typ == "TPEffect" then
			if LocalPlayer == Player then else
				Teleport(thing.Stsrt,thing.End)
			end
		elseif typ == "KillEffect" then
			KillEffect(thing.CFrame,thing.Size)
		elseif typ == "Kill" and Damage == true then
			local pos,range,parts,killeffects,ignore = thing.Pos,thing.Range,{},{},IgnoreParts(true)
			if DamageType == "Distance" then
				for i,v in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
					if v:IsA("BasePart") and v.Name ~= "Baseplate" and (v.Position - pos).Magnitude <= range*.5 and not table.find(ignore,v) then
						table.insert(parts,v)
						local Tabl = {Pos = v.CFrame,Size = v.Size}
						table.insert(killeffects,Tabl)
					end
				end
			else
				local parts1,parts2 = workspace:FindPartsInRegion3WithIgnoreList(Region3.new(pos-Vector3.new(range,range,range)*.5,pos+Vector3.new(range,range,range)*.5),ignore,5000),{}
				for i,v in pairs(parts1) do
					if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
						if v:IsA("BasePart") and v.Name ~= "Baseplate" then
							table.insert(parts,v)
							local Tabl = {Pos = v.CFrame,Size = v.Size}
							table.insert(killeffects,Tabl)
						end
					end
				end
			end
			for i,v in pairs(parts) do
				if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
					coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
						InsertP(v)
						Void(v)
					end))
				end
			end
			for i,v in pairs(killeffects) do
				if v then
					coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
						KillEffect(v.Pos,v.Size)
					end))
				end
			end
		elseif typ == "ClearTable" then
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.ClassName)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.Locked)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.Anchored)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.CanCollide)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.CanQuery)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.CanTouch)end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()table.clear(VoidTable2.Massless)end))
		elseif typ == "Reset" then
			Reset()
		elseif typ == "ResetSong" then
			Theme.TimePosition = 0
		elseif typ == "ShieldSound" then
			if thing.Type == 1 then
				Sound(CharCFrame.Torso.Position,"rbxassetid://6817149752",1,50)
			elseif thing.Type == 2 then
				Sound(CharCFrame.Torso.Position,"rbxassetid://885411326",1,50)
			end
		elseif typ == "EndScript" then
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()Loop1:Disconnect();end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()Loop2:Disconnect();end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()Keys:Disconnect();end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()DAdded:Disconnect();end))
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				pcall(function()
					for i,v in pairs(Character) do
						if typeof(v) == "Instance" then
							pcall(function()v:Destroy()end)
						end
					end
				end)
				pcall(function()
					for i,v in pairs(Hats) do
						if typeof(v.Part) == "Instance" then
							pcall(function()v.Part:Destroy()end)
						end
					end
				end)
				pcall(function()Visualizer.P1:Destroy()end)
				pcall(function()Visualizer.P2:Destroy()end)
				pcall(function()table.clear(Character)end)
				pcall(function()table.clear(Visualizer)end)
				pcall(function()table.clear(Hats)end)
				pcall(function()Shield:Destroy()end)
				pcall(function()Theme:Destroy()end)
				pcall(function()SoulPart:Destroy()end)
				pcall(function()if FakeChar~=nil then FakeChar:Destroy()end;end)
				pcall(function()
					pcall(function()
						InfoText:Destroy()
					end)
					pcall(function()
						InfoHolder:Destroy()
					end)
					InfoHolder,InfoText = nil,nil
				end)
				if LocalPlayer == Player then
					pcall(function()
						CameraPart:Destroy()
					end)
					CameraPart = nil
				end
			end))
			ScriptEnded = true
		end
	end)
end
local function ConnectEvent(Event_)
	ConnectR(Event_)
	local EventRemoval
	EventRemoval = Event_.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
		if not Event_:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			RFunction:Disconnect()
			local FoundRemote = false
			repeat
				if ScriptEnded == true then return end
				game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
				local PotentialRemote = game:FindFirstChild(Code,true)
				if typeof(PotentialRemote) == "Instance" and PotentialRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") and PotentialRemote.Name == Code then
					Remote = PotentialRemote
					FoundRemote = true
				end
			until FoundRemote
			ConnectEvent(Remote)
			EventRemoval:Disconnect()
		end
	end)
end
local FoundRemote = false
repeat
	if ScriptEnded == true then return end
	game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
	local PotentialRemote = game:FindFirstChild(Code,true)
	if typeof(PotentialRemote) == "Instance" and PotentialRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") and PotentialRemote.Name == Code then
		Remote = PotentialRemote
		FoundRemote = true
	end
until FoundRemote
ConnectEvent(Remote)
coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()while ScriptEnded == false do wait(.1)if ShieldEnabled == true then Kill(CharCFrame.Torso.Position,25)end;end;end))
function CrazyVal()
	if Multiply > 1 then
		return true
	elseif Multiply <= 1 then
		return false
	else
		return nil
	end
end

								v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
							end
						elseif v == Character.RightWing or v == Character.LeftWing then
							if HumanoidMode == true and Skin == 1 then
								v.Parent = nil
							else
								v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
							end
						elseif v == Character.homero then
							if HumanoidMode == true and UseAnim == true and Moving == false and Falling == false and Attacking == false and Animation == 5 then
								v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
							else
								v.Parent = nil
							end
						else
							v.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
						end
					end))
				end
			end
		end))
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			for i,v in pairs(Hats) do
				if v.Part and v.WeldTo and v.Offset then
					coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
						v.Part.Parent = FakeChar or workspace
						if v.WeldTo == "Head" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.Head*v.Offset:Inverse()
						elseif v.WeldTo == "Torso" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.Torso*v.Offset:Inverse()
						elseif v.WeldTo == "RightArm" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.RightArm*v.Offset:Inverse()
						elseif v.WeldTo == "LeftArm" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.LeftArm*v.Offset:Inverse()
						elseif v.WeldTo == "RightLeg" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.RightLeg*v.Offset:Inverse()
						elseif v.WeldTo == "LeftLeg" then
							v.Part.CFrame = CharCFrame.LeftLeg*v.Offset:Inverse()
						end
					end))
				end
			end
		end))
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			if typeof(FakeChar) == "Instance" then
				FakeChar.Parent = workspace
			end
		end))
		if CustomColorBoolean == false then
			if HumanoidMode == true and UseAnim == true and (Animation == 3 or Animation == 5) then
				CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255),.25)
			elseif Mode == 0 then
				CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(tick()%2.5/2.5,.5,1),.25)
			elseif Mode == 1 or Mode == 9 or Mode == 12 then
				CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(tick()%2.5/2.5,1,1),.25)
			elseif Mode == 2 then
				CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255),.25)
			elseif Mode == 3 or Mode == 7 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(0,math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255),0),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(0,255,0),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 4 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255,(math.random(0,255)/255)*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255)),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255,math.random(0,255)/255),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 6 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(tick()%2.5/2.5,1,math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness-191,0,255)/255),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromHSV(tick()%2.5/2.5,1,1),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 8 then	
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness/2,0,255/2),0,math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(170,0,255),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 10 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(255*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255),137*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255),73*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255)),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(255,137,73),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 11 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.new(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255,math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255,math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.new(1,1,1),.25)
				end
			elseif Mode == 13 then
				if Theme.IsLoaded == true and Theme.IsPlaying == true then
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(140*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255),91*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255),159*(math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness,0,255)/255)),.25)
				else
					CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.fromRGB(140,91,159),.25)
				end
			else
				CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(Color3.new(1,1,1),.25)
			end
		else
			CurrentColor = CurrentColor:Lerp(CustomColor,.25)
		end
		CurrentColor2 = CurrentColor2:Lerp(CustomColor2,.25)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			Shield.CFrame,Shield.Color,Shield.Material,Shield.Transparency = CFrame.new(CharCFrame.Torso.Position)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-Sine*.25),math.rad(-Sine*.5),0),CurrentColor,Enum.Material.ForceField,.25*math.cos(Sine/25)

			else
				Shield.Parent,Shield.Size = nil,Vector3.new()
			end
		end))
		SoulPos = SoulPos:Lerp(CFrame.lookAt(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(5*math.cos(Sine/33.341),2+2*math.cos(Sine/45.412),5*math.sin(Sine/33.341)),CharCFrame.Torso.Position),.1)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			SoulPart.CFrame = SoulPos
			SoulPart.Color = CurrentColor
			SoulAssets.Trail.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
			SoulAssets.Particles.Center.Color,SoulAssets.Particles.Square.Color,SoulAssets.Particles.Square2.Color,SoulAssets.Particles.Particle.Color,SoulAssets.Particles.Smoke.Color = ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor),ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor),ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor),ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor),ColorSequence.new(CurrentColor)
			SoulAssets.Particles.Particle.Acceleration = Vector3.new(3*math.cos(Sine/5.521),-3*math.cos(Sine/7.851),3*math.cos(Sine/9.213))
			SoulPart.Parent = workspace
		end))
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			Theme.SoundId = SoundId
			Theme.Looped = true
			Theme.PlayOnRemove = false
			Theme.Volume = 3
			Theme.PlaybackSpeed = 1
			Theme.Parent = Character.Torso
			Distortion.Parent = Theme
			Distortion.Enabled = true
			if Theme.SoundId == "rbxasset://Naw.mp3" then
				Distortion.Level = 1
			else
				Distortion.Level = 0
			end
			Distortion.Priority = 0
		end))
		local RayCast,Po = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,3,0),Vector3.new(0,-9e12,0)),IgnoreParts(false),false,true)
		if VisEnabled == true then
			Visualizer.P1.Parent,Visualizer.P2.Parent,Visualizer.P1.Color = workspace,workspace,CurrentColor
			if VisSkin == 2 then
				Visualizer.P1.Size,Visualizer.P2.Size = Visualizer.P1.Size:Lerp(Vector3.new(Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.9,0.05,Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.9),.25),Visualizer.P2.Size:Lerp(Vector3.new(Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.4,0.08,Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.4	),.25);if Skin==1 then Visualizer.P2.Color=CurrentColor2;else Visualizer.P2.Color=MainColor;end
			else
				Visualizer.P1.Size,Visualizer.P2.Size = Visualizer.P1.Size:Lerp(Vector3.new(Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.9,0.08,Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40*.9),.25),Visualizer.P2.Size:Lerp(Vector3.new(Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40,0.05,Theme.PlaybackLoudness/40),.25);if Skin==1 then Visualizer.P2.Color=CurrentColor2;else Visualizer.P2.Color=MainColor;end
			end
		elseif VisEnabled == false then
			Visualizer.P1.Parent,Visualizer.P2.Parent,Visualizer.P1.Color,Visualizer.P1.Size,Visualizer.P2.Size = nil,nil,CurrentColor,Vector3.new(),Vector3.new()
		end
		if RayCast ~= nil then
			if VisSkin == 2 then
				Visualizer.P1.CFrame,Visualizer.P2.CFrame = CFrame.new(Po)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-VisSine*10),0),CFrame.new(Po)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-VisSine*15),0)
			else
				Visualizer.P1.CFrame,Visualizer.P2.CFrame = CFrame.new(Po),CFrame.new(Po)
			end
		else
			if VisSkin == 2 then
				Visualizer.P1.CFrame,Visualizer.P2.CFrame = CFrame.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,-3-HipHeight,0))*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-VisSine*10),0),CFrame.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,-3-HipHeight,0))*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-VisSine*10),0)
			else
				Visualizer.P1.CFrame,Visualizer.P2.CFrame = CFrame.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,-3-HipHeight,0)),CFrame.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,-3-HipHeight,0))
			end
		end
	end))
end)
coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	if LocalPlayer == Player then
		local Sg = Saves.StartGui:Clone()
		local DM,Message,Warn = Sg.Dm,Sg.Message,Sg.Warn
		ApplyRandomString(Sg)
		local DMPos,MessagePos,WarnPos = DM.Position,Message.Position,Warn.Position
		DM.TextTransparency,DM.TextStrokeTransparency = 0,0
		Message.TextTransparency,Message.TextStrokeTransparency = 0,0
		Warn.TextTransparency,Warn.TextStrokeTransparency = 0,0

		Sg.IgnoreGuiInset = true
		Sg.Parent = PlayerGui

				end))

		end))
		for i=1,50 do

			Message.Position,Message.Rotation = MessagePos+UDim2.new(math.random(-i,i)*((50-i)*0.0001),0,math.random(-i,i)*((50-i)*0.0001),0),math.random(-i,i)*((50-i)*0.025)

			Warn.TextTransparency,Warn.TextStrokeTransparency = i/50,i/50

Loop1=game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(hb)
	if ScriptEnded == true then return end
	if Sine>1000000000 then Sine=0;end
	SoulNums.Square,SoulNums.Smoke = SoulNums.Square+1,SoulNums.Smoke+1
	VisSine=VisSine+.1+((math.clamp(Theme.PlaybackLoudness-191,0,255)/255)*.9)
	if LocalPlayer == Player then
		Sine=Sine+Multiply
		Remote:FireServer("Character",{Pos = Pos,PosRot = PosRot,SoundId = SoundId,Sine = Sine,Mode = Mode,Moving = Moving,Falling = Falling,Fall = Fall,Flying = Flying,TouchingFloor = TouchingFloor,HumanoidMode = HumanoidMode,HipHeight = HipHeight,MousePos = MousePos,MouseHold = MouseHold,TerrainTool = TerrainTool,VisEnabled = VisEnabled,UseAnim = UseAnim,Animation = Animation,CameraShakes = CameraShakes,CannonOnBack = CannonOnBack,LookAtCamera = LookAtCamera,CameraCFrame = CameraCFrame,CameraAngles = CameraAngles})
		if HumanoidMode == false then
			if Mode == 0 then
				Speed,HipHeight = 16,0
			elseif Mode == 1 or Mode == 3 or Mode == 4 or Mode == 5 or Mode == 6 or Mode == 7 or Mode == 9 or Mode == 11 then
				Speed,HipHeight = 50,3
			elseif Mode == 2 then
				Speed,HipHeight = 16,3
			elseif Mode == 12 then
				Speed,HipHeight = 10,0
			elseif Mode == 8 or Mode == 10 or Mode == 13 then
				Speed,HipHeight = 16,0	
			end
		else
			if UseAnim == false then
				Speed,HipHeight = 16,0
			else
				if Animation == 0 and Moving == false and Attacking == false and DoAnim == true then
					Speed,HipHeight = 16,-1.5
				else
					Speed,HipHeight = 16,0
				end
			end
		end
		MouseHold = UST("MouseButton1")
		if K("W") then
			Z = -1
		end
		if K("A") then
			X = -1
		end
		if K("S") then
			Z = 1
		end
		if K("D") then
			X = 1
		end
		if K("Q") then
			Y = -1
		end
		if K("Space") then
			Y = 1
			if Flying == false and TouchingFloor == true then
				Fall = 1+(HipHeight/3)
			end
		end
		if not K("W") and not K("S") then
			Z = 0
		end
		if not K("A") and not K("D") then
			X = 0
		end
		if not K("Q") and not K("Space") then
			Y = 0
		end
		local RayCast,Po = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray.new(RootPart.Position+Vector3.new(0,3,0),Vector3.new(0,-(6.25+HipHeight),0)),IgnoreParts(false),false,true)
		if Pos.Position.Y < workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight then
			Pos = CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,100,Pos.Position.Z)*Pos.Rotation
		end
		if Flying == false then
			if K("W") or K("A") or K("S") or K("D") then
				if RayCast == nil or Fall > .1 then
					Fall = Fall - .07
					local FakePos1,FakePos2,Rot = CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Pos.Position.Y+Fall,Pos.Position.Z),CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Pos.Position.Y+Fall,Pos.Position.Z)*CFrame.Angles(0,CameraAngles.Y,0)*CFrame.new(X,0,Z),CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)
					Rot = CFrame.lookAt(FakePos1.Position,FakePos2.Position).Rotation
					Pos = CFrame.new(FakePos1.Position)*Rot*CFrame.new(0,0,(-0.02*Speed)*Multiply)
					if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then else
						PosRot = PosRot:Lerp(Rot,.2)
					end
					TouchingFloor,Falling = false,true
				elseif RayCast ~= nil then
					Fall = 0
					TouchingFloor,Falling = true,false
					local FakePos1,FakePos2,Rot = CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Po.Y,Pos.Position.Z),CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Po.Y,Pos.Position.Z)*CFrame.Angles(0,CameraAngles.Y,0)*CFrame.new(X,0,Z),CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)
					Rot = CFrame.lookAt(FakePos1.Position,FakePos2.Position).Rotation
					Pos = CFrame.new(FakePos1.Position)*Rot*CFrame.new(0,0,(-0.02*Speed)*Multiply)
					if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then else
						PosRot = PosRot:Lerp(Rot,.2)
					end
				end
				Moving = true
			else
				if RayCast == nil or Fall > .1 then
					Fall = Fall - .07
					TouchingFloor,Falling = false,true
					Pos = CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Pos.Position.Y+Fall,Pos.Position.Z)*CFrame.Angles(0,PosAngles.Y,0)
				elseif RayCast ~= nil then
					Fall = 0
					TouchingFloor,Falling = true,false
					Pos = CFrame.new(Pos.Position.X,Po.Y,Pos.Position.Z)*CFrame.Angles(0,PosAngles.Y,0)
				end
				Moving = false
			end
			if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then
				PosRot = CFrame.Angles(0,CameraAngles.Y,0)
			end
		elseif Flying == true then
			if K("W") or K("A") or K("S") or K("D") or K("Q") or K("Space") then
				TouchingFloor,Falling,Fall = false,false,0
				local FakePos1,FakePos2,Rot = CFrame.new(Pos.Position),CFrame.new(Pos.Position)*CameraCFrame.Rotation*CFrame.new(X,Y,Z),CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)
				Rot = CFrame.lookAt(FakePos1.Position,FakePos2.Position).Rotation
				Pos = CFrame.new(FakePos1.Position)*Rot*CFrame.new(0,0,(-0.02*Speed)*Multiply)
				if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then else
					PosRot = PosRot:Lerp(Rot,.2)
				end
				Moving = true
			else
				TouchingFloor,Falling,Fall = false,false,0
				Moving = false
			end
			if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then
				PosRot = CameraCFrame.Rotation
			end
		end
		if Theme.SoundId == "rbxasset://Naw.mp3" then
			Multiply = 5
		else
			Multiply = 1
		end
	end
	CamDir = RootPart:toObjectSpace(CameraCFrame).lookVector
	if HumanoidMode == false then
		if LookAtCamera == true then
			Welds.Neck.C1 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C1,CFrame.new(0,-0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,math.rad(180)) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.asin(CamDir.x)) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin(CamDir.y),0,0),.25)
		else
			Welds.Neck.C1 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C1,CFrame.new(0,-0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,math.rad(180)) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
		end
		Welds.RightShoulder.C1 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C1,CFrame.new(-.5,.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(90),0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)

		if Mode == 12 and Moving == true and Falling == false then
			Welds.RootJoint.C1 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C1,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0.1 + 0.05 * math.cos(Sine / 6)) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
			Welds.RightHip.C1 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C1,CFrame.new(0.5,.95-.2*math.sin(Sine/12),-.15*math.sin(Sine/12)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(90),0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(-10+35 * math.cos(Sine / 12))),.25)
			Welds.LeftHip.C1 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C1,CFrame.new(-0.5,.95+.2*math.sin(Sine/12),.15*math.sin(Sine/12)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-5),math.rad(-90),0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(10+35 * math.cos(Sine / 12))),.25)
		else
			Welds.RootJoint.C1 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C1,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0 * CFrame.new(0,0,0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
			Welds.RightHip.C1 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C1,CFrame.new(0.5,1,0) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(90),0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
			Welds.LeftHip.C1 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C1,CFrame.new(-0.5,1,0) * CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-90),0) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
		end
	else
		if LookAtCamera == true then
			Welds.Neck.C1 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C1,CFrame.new(0,-0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,math.rad(180)) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.asin(CamDir.x)) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin(CamDir.y),0,0),.25)
		else
			Welds.Neck.C1 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C1,CFrame.new(0,-0.5,0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),0,math.rad(180)) * CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.25)
		end
