					elseif Animation == 4 then
						Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0*CFrame.new(0,0,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(Sine*45),0,0),.5)
						Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0*CFrame.new(0,0,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,0),.5)
						Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)*Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,.5)
						Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,0)*Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,.5)
						Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(90),0),.5)
						Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-90),0),.5)
						Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),.5)
					elseif Animation == 5 then
						Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0*CFrame.new(math.clamp(-.5*math.cos(Sine/5),-.25,.25),.25,-.37+math.clamp(.5*math.cos(Sine/2.5),-.25,.25))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15),math.rad(-math.clamp(25*math.cos(Sine/5),-15,15)),0),.5)
						Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0*CFrame.new(0,0,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-15),math.rad(math.clamp(25*math.cos(Sine/5),-15,15)/2),0),.5)
						Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,1.2,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(180),0,0)*Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,.5)
						Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,1.2,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(180),0,0)*Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,.5)
						Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1.1-.25*math.cos(Sine/5),-.5+math.clamp(math.clamp(-.5*math.cos(Sine/5),-.25,.25),-1.25,.25),-.5+.065*math.cos(Sine/2.5))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-25),math.rad(90),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-math.clamp(45*math.cos(Sine/5),-25,25)),0,0),.5)
						Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1.1-.25*math.cos(Sine/5),-.5-math.clamp(math.clamp(-.5*math.cos(Sine/5),-.25,.25),-.25,1.25),-.5+.065*math.cos(Sine/2.5))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-25),math.rad(-90),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.clamp(45*math.cos(Sine/5),-25,25)),0,0),.5)
						Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),.5)
					else
						Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0*CFrame.new(0,0,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5+2*math.cos(Sine/50)),0,0),.25)
						Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0*CFrame.new(0,0,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(1+1*math.sin(Sine/50)),0,0),.25)
						Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5+2*math.sin(Sine/50)),0,0)*Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,.25)
						Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5+2*math.sin(Sine/50)),0,0)*Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,.25)
						Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1,-.035*math.cos(Sine/50))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(95+2*math.cos(Sine/50)),math.rad(90),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-2),0,0),.25)
						Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-1,-.035*math.cos(Sine/50))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(95+2*math.cos(Sine/50)),math.rad(-90),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-2),0,0),.25)
						Welds.GunJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.GunJoint.C0,CFrame.new(0.05,-1,-0.15) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90),math.rad(0),math.rad(0)),.25)
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
	if HipHeight > 0 then
		Welds.RightWing.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightWing.C0,CFrame.new(.15,.5,.5)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(105-25*math.cos(Sine/17)),0),.25)
		Welds.LeftWing.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftWing.C0,CFrame.new(-.15,.5,.5)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(75+25*math.cos(Sine/17)),0),.25)	
	elseif HipHeight <= 0 then
		Welds.RightWing.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightWing.C0,CFrame.new(.15,.5,.5)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(105),0),.25)
		Welds.LeftWing.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftWing.C0,CFrame.new(-.15,.5,.5)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(75),0),.25)
	end
	if SoulNums.Square >= 45 then
		SoulNums.Square = 0
		SoulAssets.Particles.Square:Emit(1)
	end
	if SoulNums.Smoke >= 42 then
		SoulNums.Smoke = 0
		SoulAssets.Particles.Smoke:Emit(1)
	end
	SoulAssets.Particles.Center:Emit(1)
	SoulAssets.Particles.Particle:Emit(1)
end)
